SF State in the Media

A selection of recent stories about the San Francisco State University community that have appeared in the media.

These summaries link directly to pages published by the media outlets cited. They may offer free online access for a limited time only (e.g. one week from publication), or may discontinue live links at any time.

December

The Mercury News

12/13/2024

Harrison Coleman, alumnus and Air Force veteran, discussed how the Grateful Gatherings organization helped him with furniture after he spent several years unhoused. Grateful Gatherings is a nonprofit organization that supports unhoused individuals.

WTMJ-AM

12/13/2024

International Relations Associate Professor Anthony Pahnke discussed growing up on a farm and being a member of the Family Farm Defenders, a nonprofit dedicated to advocating for a farmer-controlled and consumer-oriented food system, on “The Mid-West Farm Report” podcast. (Clip is not available online.)

E&E News

12/12/2024

John Logan, director and professor of Labor and Employment Studies, discussed protecting federal workers should the Trump administration’s proposed Department of Government Efficiency attempt to eliminate their positions. (This article has a paywall.)

WEZI-FM

12/12/2024

Alumnus Vince Guaraldi, the jazz pianist and composer known for his score of “A Charlie Brown Christmas,” was profiled.

Yahoo!

12/12/2024

The founding artistic director of South Coast Repertory, alumnus Martin Benson, was remembered. Benson founded the theatre with fellow alumnus David Emmes in 1964. (This article was originally published by Deadline.)

Les Echos

12/9/2024

John Logan, director and professor of Labor and Employment Studies, was quoted in an article about union campaigns at multiple Starbucks locations in the U.S. (This article is in French and has a paywall.)

Sky & Telescope

12/12/2024

An X post by alumnus Tony Dunn was included in an article about the visibility of NASA’s spacecraft Lucy, which is scheduled to pass by Earth tonight. 

New York Amsterdam News

12/12/2024

Former faculty member and co-founder of the University’s Black Studies Department Sonia Sanchez was honored Dec. 9 by her alma mater, Hunter College. 

Richmond Times Dispatch; The Roanoke Times; The Citizen

12/11/2024

International Relations Associate Professor Anthony Pahnke wrote an editorial about farmland security and the Farm Bill, which aims to keep land in the hands of farmers. (This article was originally published 12/6/2024 by The Progressive Magazine. It was republished in 22 additional media outlets.)

The New York Times; Deadline

12/11/2024 – 12/12/2024

The founding artistic director of South Coast Repertory, alumnus Martin Benson was remembered. Benson founded the theatre with fellow alumnus David Emmes in 1964. (The New York Times article can be accessed through the J. Paul Leonard Library website.)

Teen Vogue; Yahoo! Lifestyle

12/11/2024

A 1984 reading at SF State by late poet and activist Nikki Giovanni was discussed in a remembrance article. Giovanni passed away 12/9/24. 

The Progressive Magazine; MSN

12/6/2024 – 12/10/2024

Associate Professor of International Relations Anthony Pahnke wrote an op-ed about how policies surrounding farming and agriculture practices in the U.S. could lead to food insecurity.

Sonoma Magazine

December 2024

Former Music Lecturer Saul Gropman, owner of Cafe La Haye in Sonoma, has announced his retirement.

Pacific Sun

12/10/2024

Jaime Jahncke, adjunct professor of Biology and director of the California Current Group at Point Blue Conservation Science, was listed as one of the researchers on a catamaran used as part of an ocean science study in the Bay Area. 

Marin Independent Journal

12/8/2024

Professor Emeritus of Secondary Education Mark Phillips wrote an op-ed about the value of encouraging adolescents to learn more about historical political figures.

Richmond Review/Sunset Beacon

12/6/2024

Student Sam Goldberg discussed the inspiration for his short film “Upstaged,” which premiered Dec. 7 at the Balboa Theatre as part of Another Hole In The Head Film Festival’s “Strictly Local” event.

San Francisco Bay Times

12/5/2024

Lecturer of Public Health Deborah Craig’s documentary “Sally!” was featured. The documentary is a biography of late Professor Emerita of Speech and Communication Studies Sally Gearhart.

The Kansas City Star

12/6/2024

Kansas City Chiefs Coach Andy Reid’s time as an assistant football coach at SF State was discussed in an article about how a professional relationship with Mike Holmgren, also a former SF State assistant football coach, contributed to his success as a coach.

12/4/2024

Student Ian Ly, guitarist for the Crying Uncle Bluegrass Band, was interviewed about his life playing music.

12/4/2024

Founding South Coast Repertory Artistic Director Martin Benson, an alumnus, died Saturday. He co-founded the theatre company with fellow alumnus David Emmes in 1964.

John Logan, director and professor of Labor and Employment Studies, discussed one-day labor strikes on an episode of the National Public radio podcast “The Indicator.”
